Ayssi comensan las paraulas de Albucasim .	 The passage translates as follows in English: When pain occurs due to cold humors infiltrating each part of the body, especially on the feet.
O, filhs, pus yeu he a vos complit aquest libre, le qual es le derier de la sciencia de medicina, per le compliment de lu so consequit la fi en lu, e per las exposicios de lu, e per las declaracios de lu, es a mi vist que yeu complesca aquel a vos am aquest tractat, le qual es partida de la operacio am ma, so es cyrurgia.	 "Dear reader, please remember to read this treatise carefully as it is the last of the science of medicine, for its completion and use in practice, and also because of the declarations made by us regarding it, it must be given attention.
Quar la operacio am ma es prostrada en nostre regio e en nostre temps de tot privada, entro que fort leu peric la sciencia de lu, e le vistigi de lu es ostat; e no romasero de lu sino alcunas petitas descripcios en les libres dels Antics, les quals mudero las mas e endevenc ad aquels error e heyssitacio entro que son clausas las entencios de lu e es elonguada la forsa de lu e l’art. And also of blood vessels and quiet places, and of the locations where excretion occurs.
E per aquo ditz Ypocras que am u nom es mot, mays en l’obra petit, e majorment en la art de la ma.	 In this context, Ypocras means "to be called" or "it is customary to call".
Mays nos ja avem dit de aquel en l’introit de aquest libre; quar qui no es scient aquo que li avem dit de anotomia, no es evacuat que no caia en error per la qual siran mortz les homes, ayssi cum yeu he vist trops de aquels, quar alscus son formatz en esta sciencia e gettan se de aquela ses sciencia e ses experiment.	 This sentence means that anatomy is essential to know in order to avoid errors and potential mistakes which could lead to death of the patients; as such understanding of this science and its experiments are vital for those who wish to master it, including doctors and surgeons alike.
Quar yeu vi un metge folh e enperit aver incidit un apostema escrophilos en le colh de una femna, e incidic alcunas arterias del colh per que fluic gran sanc entro que la femna cazec morta entre las mas de lu. E vi un autre metge que pres que el traguera una peyra d’un home le qual avia procesit en sa etat, e la peyra era gran, e venguet a lu e trayssec aquela peyra am un tros de la vesiqua, per que aquel home al tertz dia es mort.	 Another doctor prescribed a poultice to someone who had been ill for some time and the poultice was large enough that it could be placed in their abdomen as well; however they died on the third day.
E yeu ja apelat fuy a estrayre aquela, e vi que per la grandesa de la peyra e per la disposicio del malaute conogui subre lu que morira.	 You had already found it necessary to remove that, and you saw because of the size of the ulcer and due to the patient's condition that he would die.
E vi un autre metge le qual prenia stipendic de un duc de nostra terra per cyrurgia, e endeven a un crastrat negre le qual era deves lu fractura en la coyssa de lu; e perparec le metge am la sua ignorancia, estrayssec la fractura, sobre la plagua, am pulvinas e astelas am forta strectura, e no layssec a la plagua espiracio. Cove que yeu digua la qualitat dels juvamentz de aquel cauteri e dels noccumentz de lu, e en qual compleccio sia prohibit cauteri.	 That you judge the quality of young cauteries and old ones alike, and which are forbidden cauteries.
Donc dic que·l sermo de la qualitat del juvament de cauteri e del noccument de lu es sermo lonc e prolixs, e subtil per sciensa, e secret amaguat; e ja de lu a parlat gran multitut de savis, e de lu se son desacordatz, et a mi abasta un petit dels sermons de lor, temen perlonguacio.	 So I say that the treatise on quality of young cauteries and old ones is long and detailed, subtle in learning, secret in knowledge; and it reveals many secrets, and often contradicts itself, but one of its lessons is short enough for us to remember.
E donc dic que cauteri comfereys a tota compleccio universalment la qual es am materia o ses materia, exceptat dos compleccios, las quals son compleccios caudas ses materia .	 Therefore I say that cauteries are commonly at the center of all complete works on medicine or on their subjects, except for two exceptions.
En la compleccio cauda e secca am materia se desecordero; quar alcus dyssero que cauteri es juvatiu ad aquela, e les autres dyssero le contrari de aquel, que cauteri no es convenient en malautia la qual es per qualiditat e per siccitat, quar natura del foc es qualiditat e siccitat, e enconvenient es que malautia cauda e secca am aquo que es caut e sec sia sanada.	 In the dry and hard matter there is a contradiction; namely that hot cauteries are good for health but cold ones are bad because they cause dryness (from heat causing dryness, and cold causing dryness); it's convenient to have dry and hard matter when cautery and dryness are both beneficial.
E diysec aquel que ditz le contrari de aquel, que per cauteri es fayt juvament en tota malautia cauda e secca que ve en les cors dels homes, quar quan tu comparas le cors de home e las humiditatz de lu a la compleccio del foc, atrobas le cors de home freg.	 When you compare the chest of one man to that of another and contrast the moistness in them with the heat at their center, you burn away the moisture from his chest

Do not worry about the complications and the wet and dry illnesses that are present in those cases, as all doctors agree on them, and it is not advisable to perform a cautery there at once.
E sapiatz, filhs, que del secret de curacio per cauteri am foc e de la bontat de lu, so sobre cauteri am medicina comburent, es quar le foc es simple, la accio del qual no perven sino al membre le qual es cauterizat e no notz al autre membre am lu ajustat sino am petit nocument.	 It is important to remember that cautery used in conjunction with medicine for treatment purposes has complications compared to cautery alone as the heat applied may only affect the member where it was performed and does not also touch other members of the body as intended.
Mays la accio de medicina comburent perven ad aquel en les membres le qual de lu alunhat, e fort leu fa venir en le membre malautia de dificil sanacio e fort leu ausit.	 The action of medicine combined can lead to complications in the member where it was applied, and may also cause difficulty in healing in the member affected with a difficult disease or cause harm.
Mays le foc, per la sua sublimitat e de la sua substancia bontat, no fa aquo sino que superfluisca E ja es a nos conogut per experiment e per longitut de servitut de studi am l’art sobre le veritat de las causas; e per aquo yeu so excusat de la longitut del sermo E si no fos que no es legut al mieu libre en aquest pausero a vos secret amaguat am le foc, e la qualitat de la operacio de lu en les cors e de la sieua expulcio per la qual expellis las malautias, am sermo philosophic demostratiu, le qual siria acuit en las vostras pessas. E aysso no catz en vostras pessas, o, filhs, aquo no estiman sino le poble vulguar e les fols metges, so es que ad aquela malautia que es sanada per cauteri no es redicio tot temps, e pausan aquel consequen.	 And in your minds or else it is not estimated that this common ailment and the folk doctors do not cease but to the popular vulgar and the folk healers who are only cured by cauteries do not always exist, and they pause on that consequence.
E la causa no es ges ayssi quo els cuydan per aquo, quar cauteri no es sino en loc de medicina la qual altera la compleccio e esicca las humiditatz las quals son causa per que veno las dolors.	 When the cause is not external to this place, cautery should only be applied in the place of medicine that alters the complexion and causes dryness due to which pains occur.
Mays empero cauteri superflueys sobre la medicina per volicitat de la sua valitut e vertut de la sua operacio e grandesa del sieu senhor.	 However, you should apply cautery only on top of the medicine in order to improve its effectiveness and speed up its absorption into the body and enhance its healing properties.
E es possible que la sua malautia retorne en alcuna hora del temps, segon la compleccio del malaute e la locacio de la sua malautia, e la vertut de lu, e aquo que es preparat en le cors de lu de la agreguacio de las superfluitatz en lu, e aquo que es pervengut a lu en la sua acquisicio en viandas e semblantz de aquelas causas; sino que la malautia en la qual sia aministrat cauteri sia malautia subtil en membre de paucas superfluitatz e humiditatz, ayssi cum cauteri de dent per dolor e semblantz ad aquel, possible es que en lu no retorne aquela dolor, mays aquo se fa en petitz.	 It is also possible that the ailment may return at some point in time due to the composition of the patient and their location on the body, as well as the moisture and excess fluids present, which are aggravated by applying cautery; however, if cautery is administered without causing excessive moisture or dryness within the affected area, it is less likely that the pain will return.
E mays sermo vulgar es que cauteri es le derier remezi de medicina, e es sermo dreyturier, no ad aquo que els entendo en lu, quar els crezo que no es curacio que aprofieyta am medicina ni am autra causa aprop cauteri.	 It is more commonly known that cautery should be considered as the last resort in medicine, and it should not be used alone when other treatments have proven ineffective or inadequate.
E la causa es en contrari de aquo; e la entencio que cauteri es le derier remezi de medicina no es sino quan administram las manieyras de curacio en alcunas malautias, e aquelas medicinas no conferieysso, e aprop en la fi de la causa aministra hom cauteri, e aprofieyta ad aquela.	 The cause is contrary to this; in such cases, when applying curative treatments and the medications do not yield a result or prove inadequate, doctors will administer cautery at that point as well.
E lahoras de aqui cat16 que cauteri es le derier remezi de medicina, no segon la entencio la qual entendo les vulgars e trops dels fols metges.	 "The pains here referred to as 'catarrh' are due to phlegm accumulating in the passages of the body.

De cauteri de dolor de cap per frigiditat e humiditat.	 "Gout of the head due to cold and humidity.
Le capitol primier.	 "The first chapter.
Aquesta cauterizacio confereys a la humiditat e frigiditat sobre le servel accident de la qual so doas causas, so es causa de soda e multitut de flux raumatic, apelat corissa, del cap a las partidas dels huelhs e de las aurelhas fluent, e multitut de dormir, e de dolor de dentz e del guolayro, e universalment de tota malautia que ve per fregiditat, ayssi cum paraliticament, sodo e apoplexio, e semblantz en aquelas malautias. De curacio de opilacio de aurelhas.	 To cure the arrow wound
Alcunas veguadas alcus enfantz yeysso dels ventres de lors mayres no-perforatz, e aquo ja accideys en alcus homes, opilacio en le meat de la aurelha per plagua o per carn nada en aquela; e aquesta opilacio alcunas veguadas es fayta en le preon del trau de la aurelha la qual no consiec le vezement, e alcunas veguadas es en las partidas defora. De curacio de cranc.	 Treatment for gout
Ja havem dit, en la divisio, de specia de cranc e en qual manieyra es via a la curacio de lu am medicinas, e que es squivador en lu la curacio am ferr per so que no sia ulcerat; e havem dit cranc engendrat en la mayra e cautela de la curacio de lu.	 The specific treatment for gout includes using a cautery and the carefulness in applying it to prevent ulceration, as well as taking medication to cure the ailment itself.
E diyssero les antics que alcunas veguadas cranc es en loc on es possibla la eradicacio de lu, ayssi cum de cran le qual es en las mamillas o en la coyssa e a lor semblantz dels membres allocat a estrayre tot aquel, e majorment quan es comensant petit.	 We would recommend cauterizing the affected area if it is possible to eliminate gout completely, as well as cauterizing any veins or cysts that may be present in the location where the treatment will take place, and also cauterizing anywhere on the body's extremities (such as hands, feet, etc.).
Mays quan es antiquat e es gra, no cove que te propries a lu, quar yeu non pogui sanar de aquel alcu ni no he vist autre, ni que sia pervengut ad aquo.	 When it is old and severe, you should not apply heat to it, as there may be no way to heal that part of the body or prevent further damage to it, neither should it be applied at all, nor can it ever be put on again.

The operation on it is when you're doing as recommended, that means placing a bandage over the affected area and wiping away the black bile from the veins of a patient, applying pressure to it if there are visible wounds.

"The patient is prepared for the operation, and when it comes to closing the incision, they instruct that any opening or breach of any sort should not occur; and by performing a thorough examination within this period of time, no reason will be found for their occurrence.
E layssa correr le sanc, e no abscidas aquel leugierament, e exprem les locs, e abstergeys le sanc gros tot am la tua ma o am instrument am le qual es a tu possible dels instruments. De curacio de ydropici.	 "Treatment for dropsy.
Nos ja havem recomtat, en la divisio, de las specias de ydropici de l’aygua, e les senhals de quascuna especia, de la curacio de lu am medicinas.	 "We recommend in division, among the various species of dropsy and their symptoms, to give treatment with medicines.
E aquela la qual es curada am ferr no es sino la specia de althitas sola, e no es aproximat am ferr a la specia de timpanistres ni a la especia de yposarcha, quar aquo es mortal. E quan tu ja has medicat aquesta especia de ydropici timpanistre am medicinas e no comfereys la tua medicacio, lahoras considera, quar si al malaute ja es conseguida debelitat, o es am aquel autra malautia otra ydropici, ayssi cum si es en lu tos o cos de ventre e semblant ad aquels, lahoras guarda te que no le mediques am ferr, quar temor es sobre aquo. E aprop cura aquela am la curacio de las plaguas, e cum inscideyses les fiels, mundifica aquela e restaura la plagua entro que sia consolidada; quar le ciphac es contrayt e no es ajustada la eminencia de ruptura.	 Adjust the flap to cover it and seal it closed if it has been cut open or injured in any way, ensuring that both ends are tightly secured together, as the stomach is being sutured and not allowing separation of the edges or tearing of the incision.
E cauteri es milhor en aquest loc, quar es pus propda a salut.	 The cautery should be applied gently in this area to avoid pain.
Capitol .lxviii.	 Chapter eighty-five of the Capitol.
De mollificacio de la codena dels testiculs.	 Treatment for testicular hydrocele.
Motas veguadas la codena dels testiculs en alcus homes es mollificada per aysso quar las carns que so entre aquela son mollificadas, e es fedat le reguardament de lu.	 The hydrocele is treated by squeezing the testicles between the thighs to ensure that they are both softened and the scrotum is gently massaged.
Adonc necessari es ad aquel que es preguat en la curacio de lu que fassa jazer le malaute segon le sieu dos, e enscida tota la codena la qual es mollificada sobre la codena natural; e aprop que ajuste doas labias am la sutura. De castracio.	 Castration
Sapias que castratio en nostre ley es excomengada, mays per causa es legut a mi que·m remembre de lu en aquest libre; e no es necessaria la rememoracio de lu sino per doas manieyras, de las quals es la una per so que aquo sia en la sciensa del metge quan es enterroguat de aquela, que sapia la curacio de lu al qual accideys; e l’autra manieyra es que nos motas vetz havem necessitat de castracio de autras bestias per les juvamentz nostres per aquelas, ayssi cum de motos, e de bocs, e de porcs, e de semblantz a las bestias.	 Castration is forbidden in our law except for two reasons: first of all so that the doctor knows how to treat it when he discovers it; and second, so that our servants do not need to castrate these animals for us from childhood onwards as they are taught by others
E donc dic que castracio es fayta en dos manieyras: o per atrissio, o per fissura a seccio.	 And therefore it is said that castration should be done in two ways: either through the flesh or through a slit section
Mays en aquela que es fayta per atrissio, la via de la opera es que nos fassam cezer la bestia en aygua cauda entro que·ls genetius de lu sian mollificatz e sian linhitz e que pendan.	 And in that way the operation is performed so we make the animal's castration through a small slit to prevent the genitals from being injured and ensure their generation remains healthy and intact
E aprop pren aquels am la tua ma entro que sian resols e no apparescan dejos le tocament.	 And then apply your hand over it, making sure not to scratch it
Mays en castracio fayta per fissura e seccio, cove que tu tenguas la bestia e premas la codena dels testicols de lu am la ma senestra.	 And in castration done through a slit and section, you have the animal and place your hand over its testicles to prevent injury
E aprop lia le suspensori, e inscideys sobre quascun huou am una seccio entro que dos huous proceseysso.	 Apply pressure, and ensure that no harm is done as a result of the process.
E aprop inscideys aquels pus que auras quascu excorjat.	 When a person's joint pain is caused by cold humors that infiltrate each part of the body, and when there are pains in the feet?
E no leysses sobre aquels del ciphac alcuna causa, sino le ciphac subtil le qual es sobre les vazes.	 If it's not about joints but rather the cause is unclear, then look for subtle signs that may be related to veins
E aquesta manieyra de castracio es milhor la qual es fayta per atrissio, quar atrissio fort leu layssa alcuna causa dels testicols per que la bestia desira coyt.	 This cautery procedure is better when performed by a skilled practitioner because the incision can cause severe harm to the testicles if not done properly, as indicated in that sentence.
E aprop cura la plagua entro que sia sanada.	 Cure the fistula completely.

De curacio de alratica.	 Treatment for the ulcer
Alratica es que le conh de la femna no sia perforat, o sia le trauc petit.	 If the woman's vagina is not perforated or split.

Mays si la oppilacio es per carnada, lahoras suspen aquela am unci, e inscideys aquela.	 When the itching occurs due to a carbuncle, it is customary for doctors to suspend that abscess and scratch that part

La forma de cristeri gran e pauc:	 Large and small cautery tools.

Capitol primier.	 The first chapter.
Summae et collectiones ex esse fracturae ossium, ex eis quarum praemissio necessaria est, antequam incipiamus rememorationem membrorum fraftorum et diversorum si uniuscuiusque.	 Bones and joints broken in many places are necessary before we begin to mention the injuries of various members.
Cove donc que diguam en le prohemi de aquest capitol las summas del sermo; e les capitols al entendament dels quals en le comensament es forsat le artifexs e a stacio sobre la veritat de aquels; so es vos e aquels que so promptz que sapian o aprenguan aquesta art nobla autres de vos.	 Therefore, please mention in the following chapters all of the remedies mentioned earlier, along with their reasons and explanations as to why they work or do not work for you, both those that are known to you already and those that you have yet to learn about this noble art.
E donc dic que quan accideys a alcu fractura o dislocacio o torcio o cazement, lahoras cove que tu te coytes al comensament am fleubotomia o aleyar aquel, o quascu ensemps, si no prohibeys alcuna causa, ayssi cum debelitat de vertut, o es aquel al qual accideys effant, o viel en decrepitat, o es temps de vehement calor, o de vehement freg.	 Therefore, if any bone or joint fractures, dislocates, twists, or sprains you will seek out a physician immediately to apply remedies for it, unless there is no cause, then go ahead and do the remedy anyway, as that may help prevent injury further from happening.
E aprop sia content en vianda sieua de erbas frejas e de carns de auzels e de crabotz; e prohibem carns grossas e umplir si de viandas e de tota vianda que umple las venas de sanc, entro que siras segurat de apostema caut, e si no temes efusio de materia al membre.	 And so that you may consume herbs and fruits of various kinds and crabs; and prevent the grosser ones from entering into your veins or swelling in such a way as to burst an artery unless you are certain it will not cause any harm, do not take them if you're afraid they might enter into the member.
E lahoras retorne le malaute al sieu regiment primier am le qual corr costuma de lu.	 When a patient's gout has returned to its first course, it must be treated as before.
E donc cum le os trencat comensa esser restaurat, lahoras cove que·l malaute sia pascut de viandas nutritivas de nutriment mot e gros e greu en les quals sia viscositat, ayssi cum so viandas faytas de froment cueyt am aygua, e ris, e caps, e pes, e ventres de vacas, e huous, e peys fresc, e vi gros e semblants ad aquels, e am aquest regiment es fayta coagulacio de fractura pus leugierament e miels.	 When the gouty attack has started anew, it is customary to treat him with nutritious foods such as soups, vegetables, and meats that are thick and heavy in order to thicken their viscid nature, by giving them water and other fluids, and also dressing the foot with cold ointments and poultices.
E sapias que les osses trinquatz quan so en les homes que so en la primiera vilura e en los decrepitz, no es possible que sian continuatz e sian consolidatz segon lur natura per la exsiccacio dels membres de lor.	 It is known that the bones will weaken when they are in a state of dryness due to their nature's absorption and consolidation after the first attack has already occurred, making them weaker as time progresses.
E son consolidatz e continuatz segon lor natura tot temps per la exsiccacio de aquels membres, e so continuatz e consolidatz aquels que so de lor en la fi de la lenitat, ayssi cum les osses dels petitz effantz.	 They continue to weaken and consolidate over time due to the dryness of their members, just like the bones from pets deteriorate in this condition.
Mays empero natura ajusta e amnecteys sobre le os trencat de tota partida alcuna causa semblant a glut en le qual es grossitut que adhereys e strenh aquel entro que so ensemps conglutinatz e liatz ensemps, entro que venen la fi de fortitut e de fermesa, ayssi cum foc al comensament, entro que denguna causa no prohibeys aquel de las suas obres.	 Nature adjusts and increases the adhesion of the gouty attack so that it becomes thicker as time goes on, causing stiffness in the joints until its end comes, just like at the start when there is not a cause to prevent the gout from continuing its attacks.
E per aquesta causa es necessari que pauses las viandas del malaute, viandas en las quals so gravitat e viscozitat e grosseza, ayssi cum havem dit.	 For this reason it is necessary to stop feeding the patient with foods that are thick and viscous and heavy in order to avoid worsening their condition as time goes on.
Mota diversitat de fractura segon diversitat del membre.	 Diversity of fracture following diversity in member
E sapias que las specias de fractura son diversas segon la diversitat dels membres, quar fractura del os de la camba es diversa de la fractura del os del cap; e la fractura del os del pietz es divers de la fractura del os del dos; e semblantment totz les autres membres son diverses entre lor.	 The types of fractures vary depending on the diversity in members, where a fracture of the leg is different from a head bone fracture, and a breastbone fracture differs from an arm bone fracture, etc., as each member has its own type of fracture
E yeu venc am rememoracio de tota specia de fractura, expausada en le sieu capitol distincta del autre.	 Remember all types of fractures mentioned separately in their respective specific sections.
Mota diversitat de fractura en si meteyssa.	 Diversity of fracture in this treatise.
E son diversificadas las specias de fractura del os en lor meteyssas; quar es fayta fractura arcuada otra aquo que accidan en lu stellas; e alcunas veguadas es fayta fractura segon la longitut del os: e so las fracturas de lu satagia e astelhas e addicios procedentz e no-procedentz, ayssi cum es fayt en la pena quan es preparada a escriure, e es fractura am plagua e disrupcio en le cap, e es fractura fissura petita.	 The types of fractures for each bone are explained separately; curved fractures, such as those occurring in the arm, and certain wedge-shaped fractures that follow their length, these different from those that occur without procedure or not followed by it, just like in writing, a tear at the base and disruption in the head.
E a tota specia es engen o turment propri en restauracio de lu segon que vindra rememoracio de lu distincta en les sieus locs.	 Each type is unique for restoration of it depending on remembrance separately from their locations
Mota senhal de fractura del os.	 Sentence about fracture bone.
E per aquo es conoguda fractura del os: es tortuositat de lu, e de aquel eminencia e appericio de lu al sentiment, e so de lu quan compremes aquel am la tua ma.	 The sentence means that the torturous nature of a bone fracture includes the suddenness and sharpness experienced by its victims when it strikes their hands or heart.
E donc quan no es en le loc tortuositat apparent ni so no es feyt deves le tieu tocament quan toques le os am agitacio e le malaute no atroba gran dolor, lahoras no es aqui fractura.	 When the torturous nature is not visible or if it does not strike you immediately when touching bone with movement and the victim does not experience great pain, then there is no fracture.
Habantz es possible que sia tortuositat o petita fissura, adon no cove que tu mauguas aquel am la tua ma e am compressio de tot; habantz pausa sobre lu de las medicinas de las quals ve rememoracio aprop aquel moment le qual conveneys al loc; e aprop sia streyt per strictura subtil.	 When there is a tortuous or small fissure, you must gently apply your hand and compression of the whole; hold it in place over the medicine that remember to do so at that moment where appropriate tightness can be adjusted; and then proceed with subtle restraint.
E sapias que·l loc quan es arcuat e no es scindit en dos o otra aquo que no accidan en lu satagie, cum es remauguda tota partida de la sua compar, lahoras cove que comenses de la tua hora a rectificacio de lu habantz que a lu accida apostema caut.	 When the location is curved and not divided into two or more parts, you must begin from your right hand to correct it by gently pressing down on each part separately as needed; otherwise, if it is all one piece, you should start with gentle pressure applied evenly over its entire surface.
E si a lu accida apostema caut, lahoras layssa aquel per alcus dias entro que cesse le apostema; e aprop engualha aquel segon quascuna manieyra que podes de levitat e de engen.	 If the corrective measure has been applied and there is no further reduction in the size of the ulcer as a result, it's time to apply pressure for at least two weeks more until the ulcer closes; otherwise, if one or both hands are lifting you up from bed due to reduced strength, you should try gentle levitation exercises.
E sapias que restauracio de lu e agulacio de lu es pus leugiera que del os en le qual accideysso sathagie.	 The restoration of the ulcer and the cauterization of it may be easier if you do so in a place that is lower than your usual position; otherwise, make sure to maintain this same position as much as possible.
E aprop strenh aquel segon que vindra la rememoracio de lu.	 And afterwards hold the remembered position for as long as possible.
Mays si en le os so satagias, lahoras es necessaria extencio de aquest membre trencat de doas partz, si es la ma o le pe; o am la tua ma si le membre es petit; o am doas cordas o am una corda e la ma.	 If the member is cut into two parts, it may be necessary to remove both hands or a hand and one leg depending on which part of the limb was amputated (hand or foot); otherwise, if you have only one arm, use both legs together as long as possible; in any case do so with two strong legs.
E sia la tua posicio am la qual pauses le membre loc engual segon la sua figura natural, mentre que las partidas so extandudas del membre trenquat, lahoras te perforsa que fassas retornar aquelas addicios am engen e segon quascuna manieyra que poyras en lor locs.	 When the part of a limb is relaxed and in accordance with its natural shape, while the veins are expanded from that limb, you should apply pressure to restore those vessels at their locations.

Do not apply pressure to the patient's body for any injury or surgery, and perform it on both hands together as per instructions given earlier.
E cove que en aquela hora aprofitablament tu toques am la tua ma aquel, e si vezes aqui alcuna causa diversa, rectifiqua aquel e enguala aquel per la quantitat de la tua vertut.	 When you have touched your hands together in this favorable moment and if there is any cause to rectify or adjust them according to the amount of experience that you have.
E exquiva vehement extenssio e compressio, ayssi cum fan mots fols metges que motas veguadas fan accidir apostema caut per la sua operacio, o fan accidir contraccio en le membre ayssi cum havem vist aquo per la operacio de lor motas veguadas.	 Exertion and compression like those of the other physicians who act in this way for their operation or contraction on a limb as seen with their previous operations.
E aprop annecteys, aprop equacio e decent operacio e strictura de aquel membre, e repaus e tranquilitat; amoneste le malaute sobre aquo e fay le squivar que no maugua aquel en la hora de las suas vigilias e del sieu dormir, e ves la sua revolucio e agitacio, e deves la sua egestio, e deves totz les sieus movementz am tota la sua vertut; e aguarda se que la posicio del membre sia posicio am la qual sia asegurada la dolor, la qual causa es quar quan sent en la disposicio de la posicio del membre delor o lesio; lahoras cove que permutes aquel ad autra disposicio de aquela am la qual non senta dolor; e guarda am aquo que la posicio de lu aquela sia dreyta e engual, per so que al membre non accida tortuositat quan es restaurat. E la qualitat de la strictura del membre tranquat es aquela que yeu recomti; per que sapias que·ls membres trencatz so diversificatz en lor parvitat e en lor grandeza e en la forma de aquels.	 When the member is in a state of rigor mortis, you should recommend that

Capitol .xvi.	 Chapter Sixteen

Capitol .xvii.	 Chapter seventeen
De la fractura del talo e dels osses del pe e dels ditz.	 Of fractures in the bones and joints of the feet and fingers

Mays si claudicacio e nodacio son recentz, lahoras cove que sian enbrocatz am aygua tebeza en la qual so coytas erbas mollificantz, ayssi cum son fuelas de altea e razitz de lu, e mellilot, e semblantz ad aquels; e sia fayt a lu emplastre am emplastre mollificatio ayssi cum dyallaquilon ben fayt; o que sia preza mucillage de razit de altea e sia contucida am gray de gualina o am oli de cirami, e sia emplastrat am aquel; o que sian prezes figuas grassas e sian trissadas am fems de colom, e semblantz ad aquels de las medicinas que son nompnadas amermans consolidacio.	 If recent claudication and nodication occur, then the pain from these causes the body to be held tight by water that makes them more frequent than before, such as the fuel of fire and air, earth, and water elements, and metal; also a fiery element which holds it in place with its fiery influence.
E alcunas vetz es dissolvuda am assidua fricacio leugiera que sia am las mas humidas, e sia administrat movement del membre a tota partida en totas horas.	 Some of the fluid is dissolved by very humid air that makes it to be most humid, and movement of the member is completely stopped in all hours.
Mays si tortuositat ja es anada denant e es fayta fort e convertida es en peyra e provocada es necessitat a curacio de lu am ferr, lahoras cove que sia le pus desus cecsat e la continuacio del os sia dissolvut, e sia inscidit aquo que superflueys de nodacio de aquel meteys am le os am inscissoris subtils, e sia aministrada facilitat en aquel am sollicitut e studi. Capitol .xxiii.	 Chapter 33.
De sermo en dislocacio.	 On dislocation.
Dislocacio es eyssiment de alcuna de las juncturas del sieu loc, per que es prohibida de movement, e es orrezada la figura del membre, e fa venir sobre le malaute dolors e lesios grans.	 The joint is dislocated from its place, which is forbidden to move, and the figure of the member is distorted, causing large injuries
Donc quan accideys ad alcu dislocacio, lahoras cove tantost perforsar que sia reduzit, e no tarde aquela reduzir, quar si es tardada, le loc es apostemat e fort leu am aquo es fayta dificil la reduccio de dislocaccio.	 Therefore when a dislocation occurs, the pains are very severe and if delayed in reducing it, the joint is often immobilized and recovery of dislocation becomes difficult.
E per aysso no cove que sia maugut ni stendut en la hora de la apostemacio, quar motas veguadas fa venir spasme e dolors ledentz.	 Therefore, do not make it too tight or stiff during the immobilization period as spasms and pain may come
Mays quan aquo accideys, lahoras cove que tu te coytes a la flaubotomia del malaute, e aprop sia layssat entro que repause le apostema; e aprop le membre sia embrocat am aygua cauda e oli, e aprop sia reduzit am facilitat.	 If that occurs, the doctor may recommend an incision of the abscess and place it under water to reduce swelling and apply heat or cold pack to relieve pain and facilitate reduction.
E tot membre sia curat am aquo del qual la rememoracio vindra en son loc.	 In other words, once a member is healed in its place, memory returns there as well.
E yeu ja e ordenatz les capitols de dislocacio segon que es precedit en fractura; de la partida del cos pus sobirana entro a la partida pus dejos.	 You will also order the bones of dislocation after it has been preceded by a fracture, from the beginning of the body to the end of the legs.

De curacio de dislocacio de la mandibula dejos.	 Treatment for dislocated jaw disorder
So dislocadas las doas mandibulas si no tart; e la dislocacio de amdos es fayta segon una de dos manieyras: que o son remaugudas de lurs locs per pauca remocio, e so mollificadas un petit; o so dislocadas per entiera dislocacio e complida, entro que sian mollificadas a la partida de la junctura entro que corro saliva del malaute e que no puesca tenir aquela ni puesca claure la sua boca, e la lengua de lu sia envolopada en sa paraula.	 One option is to gently reduce the jaw from its place with little effort and so soften them slightly; or you may dislocate it completely into another position where saliva flows out of the mouth without closing that hole nor closing your lips, and your tongue be covered by word.
Mays quan la dislocacio de lu es pauca, lahoras en las majors disposicios retorna per si an pauca causa.	 When the dislocation of it occurs rarely, then the pains return to a lesser extent if at all.
Mays si la dislocacio es entiera e complida, lahoras cove que sia administrada reduccio de lu leugierament, e no sia tardada de tot.	 If the dislocation is severe and complete, then it should be treated with reduction of the gout immediately, not delayed at all.

E donc cum retornam e so engualadas, e es clausa la boca del malaute e no es mollificada, lahoras pausa sobre aquelas polvils de drap am cerot, e sia fayt de cera e oli rozat; e aprop sia liat am facilitat am liamens mols. The patient lies on their back, and the head of them is between two arms, in order that none may touch either with a right or left hand; therefore no cause should be made except for bringing relief to severe pain.
E aquo sia aministrat am facilita, e no trebalhe sobre la apercio de la boca deves la comestio e beure e ocitatio, entro que la mandibula sia nozada e sanada.	 It is administered in a simple way and nothing should be given to the patient's mouth except for food, drink, and breath through their nose, as long as the mouth remains closed and healed up.
E si es dificil la reduccio de duas mandibulas quan so dislocadas en alcuna hora e no so convertidas als lors locs, lahoras motas veguadas accideysso febres e soda assidua, e fort leu es alerguat le ventre del malaute, e fort leu e vomeys colera pura. De la reduccio de la dislocacio del muscle.	 The reduction in care at the extremity of the affected muscle.
Sapias que·l muscle no es dislocat sino segon tres manieras, de las quals es la una que sia dislocat a la partida del titillic a la partida dejos.	 You know that the muscle is not dislocated but rather removed in three ways, one of which is to remove it at the beginning of the thread and end of it.
E la segonda es que sia dislocat a la partida desus del muscle, e aquo es fayt tart; e no es dislocat a las partidas detras per la spalla; e no es dislocat a las partidas denant per les nervis.	 The second way is to remove it at the beginning of the tendon and end of the muscle, which is called a lateral dislocation, while the third method involves removing it behind the shoulder and in front of the nerves, which is called an anterior dislocation.
E majorment es dislocat e defora eyssit a las partidas dejos deves le titillic, e majorment en aquels dels quals las carns son paucas, leugierament es dislocat; mays en aquels en les quals so motas carns, es eyssit fora am dificultat. "Place the patient on their back and raise their hips up off the table.

De curacio de dislocacio del coyde.	 The treatment of dislocation of the thigh

Capitol .xxviii.	 When joint pain is caused by cold humors that infiltrate each part of the body, it is customarily called gout by doctors
De curacio de dislocacio de malassen, so es de la junctura que es entre·l bras e la ma.	 In case of dislocation or swelling due to pain, place the joint between the arms and hand.
Malassen de la ma alcunas vetz es deslocada, e la reduccio de la dislocacio de lu es leugiera, e·l contrari es de las autras juncturas, mays empero cove que sia velocitat en la reduccio de lu en la hora en la qual es deslocada, denant que le loc sia apostemat o que accida en lu apostema caut. De curacio de anca dislocada.	 Treatment of dislocated bones
Sapias que la junctura del ancha e la junctura del muscle no endeve sino dislocacio tant solament, e no accideys ad aquelas aquo que accideys a las autras juncturas de petita remocio e concavitat.	 It is only the joint of the tendons and the joint of the muscles that can be dislocated, but not those at which accidents occur in joints with small recess and depression.
E la junctura de la ancha es dislocada segon quatre manieyras, quar es dislocada a las partidas dedintz, o a las partidas defora, o a las partidas denant, o a las partidas detras.	 The joint of the tendons is dislocated after four days, which it occurs at the front of the knee or behind it, or on one side and on the other side, or in the morning and in the afternoon.
E majorment es dislocada a las partidas dedintz, e pauc a las partidas denant o a las partidas detras.	 It is most often dislocated at the front of the knee, but less so at the front during the day or behind it.
E senhal de la dislocacio de lu a las partidas de dintz es quar, quan tu ajustas la camba del malaute sana am la malaute, es pus longua e·l denolh es pus heminent que de la sana, e·l malaute no pot doblar le sieu pe deves le lenguonar, e es le loc que siec le lengonar apostemat de apostema caut, per so que·l cap de la coyssa ja es pervengut aqui.	 When the dislocation of it to the front of the knee is fixed by adjusting a bandage on the thigh as well, its duration and intensity decrease compared to when you straighten out your leg, because the thigh cannot bend at that time, so the head of the joint will not be protruded here.
E·l senhal de aquel al qual accideys dislocacio es a las partidas defora, es que les accidentz de lu so contraris ad aquest accident.	 When an injury occurs in which joint movements are painful it is customary to call that gout.
E senhal de aquel al qual accideys dislocacio a las partidas denant es quar expan la camba sieua segon compliment, mays empero no dobla aquela ses dolor que es en le denol, e si se perforsa ad anar e no pot sobre aquo a las partidas denant; e la urina de lu es retenguda e l’engonar de lu es apostemat, e deves la ambulacio de lu sobre le talo.	 When an injury occurs in which joint movements are painful it is customary to call that gout and extend the bladder of the patient so as not to double that pain and if necessary go up to the patient's head; and urine from the patient should be retained, and the hand placed on his forehead.
E senhal de aquel al qual accideys dislocacio a las partidas detras es que no expande le denol, ni no puesca doblar aquel denant que doble le engonar, e la camba de lu es pus breva que l’autra, e l’engonar es mollificat, e·l cap de la coyssa es deves aquel loc.	 When an injury occurs in the back part of which joint movements are painful it is customary not to extend that pain and not to double that pain with another one; the bladder of the patient should be short so as not to have a second, its forehead is relaxed and the head placed there.
Mays reduccio de las specias de aquesta dislocacio es que tu consideras, lahoras, si la dislocacio es vetusta et antiqua, que ja es anticada am le havent aquela aprop tu aministras reduccio de lu e roman segon la sua disposicio, lahoras no es en aquela curacio de tot; e adonc no cove que en aquela sia fayta prosompcio.	 The remedy for this injury is that you consider the matter to be old and ancient, and already treated by the physician with a reduction of it and then on its disposition, unless they are in such care, or when there is any fault; but if nothing else occurs you should do that again.
Mays en aquel del qual la dislocacio es recent, e es una de las quatre specias de dislocacio, lahoras te coyta ad aquo que volvas la junctura e extendas aquela a las partidas dedintz e a las partidas defora, e mau aquela a la dextra e sinistra, quar fort leu retorna e no indigeys de autra cura.	 If the injury is recent and one of the four kinds then you should apply that to the joint movements extending it on both sides inward and outward, left and right; which is very good for returning blood flow but not necessary to do anything else as a cure.

Mays en la reducio propria, quan es dislocacio a la partida defora, cove que·l malaute jaga sobre pug segon que havem recomtat en le havent gelbozitat; e sia strenhut le liament sobre la camba malauta propriament e sobre le pietz de lu. Mays cove que·l malaute jagua sobre les sieus latz sa quetament.	 The patient lies on their side so that their back is flat.

E si la dislocacio es a las partidas detras, lahoras no cove que·l malaute sia extendut a las partidas dejos, e es elevat sobre la terra; habantz cove que sia pausat sobre causa dura, ayssi cum cove le eyssament si l’ancha de lu es dislocada a las partidas defora, segon aquo que havem dit del jasement de lu sobre dos anchas; e es sobre la sua cara e les liamentz sian extendutz, segon que havem dit, no ha guayre. E aprop deslia le liament e l’empastre, e compara la una camba am l’autra.	 Then remove the binding and incision, and compare one leg to the other

E aprop deslia aquel, e fay aquel tardar en ambulacio sobre quascu per alcus dias, entro que sia confortat.	 Then remove the second one, tighten it again if necessary to prevent movement during this period, until you are comfortable.
Capitol .xxxii.	 The twenty-second chapter
De curacio de dislocacio del denolh.	 Discussion on dislocation of the knee
Le denolh es dislocat segon tres manieyras, quar es dislocat a las partidas defora, e a las partidas dedintz, e a las partidas dejos mays a las partidas detras; e a las partidas denant no es dislocat.	 The knee is dislocated in the front three times, and to the sides outside it. Inside one side of it, inside the other side also, and behind none of them.
E le senhal de dislocacio de lu es que comandes al malaute que aplique la sua camba am la coyssa; lahoras sapias que·l denol es dislocat.	 When a dislocation occurs, command the patient to apply their bandage over the affected area; you will understand that it has been dislocated.
E la restauracio de totas las manieyras de lu es que fassas cezer le malaute dreyt, enayssi que ja extenda la sieua camba, si pot sobre aquo; adherir le tieu dos a la cara de lu, e pausa le pe de lu entre les tieus pes; e aprop fay adherir le denol de lu am las tuas palmas, e rete aquelas entre les tieus ditz sobre le denolh de lu am fortaleza, e autre ministre extenda le sieu pe entro que·l denol retorne a son loc.	 The restoration of all the manicuries (nails) on his body is that you shall ask the patient to straighten the bandage, if possible; and place it over her face, between their feet, and fix it against the back of the hand with your thumbs; then extend the bandage further towards the dislocation site for support, another servant to extend it into its original position once the dislocation has returned.
E senhal de reddicio de lu es que la sua camba adharesca am la coyssa am levitat no-laboroza.	 The relief of this (patient) is that their bandage remains attached to the affected area with as little effort as possible.
E aprop emplastra aquel e fay adhirir la camba am la coyssa, e aprop lia aquelas emsemps am una benda per tres dias o per quatre, e aprop deslia aquelas.	 Place it and fasten it to the affected area, and let these servants continue for three or four days, depending on their condition.
E no uze le malaute de ambulacio per alcus dias, entro que sia sanat e cofortat.	 The patient should be moved from bed during those days until they recover health and strength.
Mays si la reduccio de lu a tu es excusada, lahoras aministra fort extencio am liamentz dels quals en la curacio de la hancha precedit narracio.	 If the reduction of him is excused for any reason related to previous treatment, we will provide extra care during his recovery period.
Capitol .xxxiii.	 Chapter xxxiii
De la curacio de la dislocacio del talo.	 Of the treatment of dislocation of the leg.
Le talo alcunas veguadas es remaugut per petita remocio, e alcunas veguadas es dislocat segon compliment, e la dislocacio de lu es fayta o a las partidas dedintz o a las partidas deforo.	 The leg has certain movements that are corrected by slight correction, and others have movements that require dislocation in the second attempt; and dislocation of him is done either to his front or to the back.
E le senhal de la dislocacio de lu es que vezes le talo imflat procedent a la partida a la qual es dislocat.	 When the dislocation occurs, it often means that this body part has been displaced
Mays la curacio de la remocio de lu es de leugiera reddicio, e es que sia extendut am facilitat am las mas e sia engualhat entro que retorne.	 The care of the broken bone is to rest it, and it's recommended to stretch it gently while keeping in mind that you need to remain still
Mays en la curacio de lu quan es dislocat segon compliment, cove que fasses cezer le malaute dreyt, e tengua aquel un ministre fort e valent de la partida detras del dos de aquel en le mieg loc de lu.	 When the dislocation occurs for a second time, do not try to straighten it immediately, and keep an arm behind your back while doing so
E aprop te tu am la tieua ma dreyta le pe de la pus sobirana part, e am la tua ma sinistra de la part pus dejos del pe en le loc de la cavilha.	 Place the right foot on the most injured part of your body and place your left foot behind it in the hollow of your elbow.
E aprop atira le pe a tu am la tua ma dreyta, e aprop am la sinistra per dos veguadas, e aprop exten am la sinistra; e empelleys le pietz del pe am la dreyta deves la camba ses trebalh.	 Place your right foot on top of it, and place the left foot two steps away to either side, extending the left foot too; then pull back towards you the toes of both feet
E fay aquo doas veguadas segon que havem comtat.	 Do this after performing as previously mentioned.
E aprop empelleys le pietz del pe a la camba la tersa veguada, e tu es a la cavilha.	 Place the toes of your right foot towards the back step and go to the hollow of your elbow.
Donc si retorna en una veguada o en dos segon aquesta manieyra, e si vezes le pe engualhat, es bo; e sino, lahoras sobre lu itera la operacio, quar aquel retorna.	 So if after one or two steps you notice this position is uncomfortable, and the foot becomes painfull, then stop and call for assistance, otherwise continue the operation until they come back.
Mays si a tu es prohibida la reduccio de lu am aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras fay jaser le malaute sobre le sieu dos sobre terra, e estrenh un paysel mot en terra fermat, e que caja entre las coyssas de lu, e tu ja has envolopat sobre lu drap per so que no ledesca le malaute.	 If you are prohibited from reducing the dislocation as advised earlier, lie down the body part on its two sides flat on the ground and place a cushion between your thighs, then cover it with a blanket to prevent the body part from moving.
E aprop le ministre de lu tengua las suas coyssas, e aprop autre ministre extenda le pe am las suas mas o am liament que lie sobre le col del pe; e aprop extenda aquel quascun ministre contre extencio del sieu par, e le payssel sia extant entre las coyssas del malaute retinent aquel, per so que·l cos de lu no sia atirat a las partidas dejos deves la sua extencio.	 "The first servant must place themselves between the patient's thighs and support their head on cushions placed under them.
E aprop le metge enguala la dislocacio am las sieuas mas, e autre ministre tengua la coyssa sana a las partidas dejos, quar la dislocacio retorna am la facilitat.	 "The doctor must stretch the healthy leg behind the patient's back and support their head on cushions placed under them.
E donc cum retorna la dislocacio e es declarada a tu la sanetat de la reduccio de lu, lahoras pausa emplastre e extrenh aquela am liamentz fortment, e ligua le pe am liament a la camba.	 "When the dislocation is corrected and declared healthy by the doctor, they will place the person back on their good leg and support their head with an arm placed under their armpit.
E cove que temes o te guardes dels nervis les quals so detras sobre le talo, per que le liament sobre aquel no sia vehement e leda aquel fortment.	 "Ensure that you protect the nerves behind your back as they are being worked on to prevent any excessive pressure or injury.
E aprop layssa aquel per dos dias o per tres; e si le liament es mollificat, extrenh aquel.	 "Support him for two days or three, and if it becomes soft, stretch it further.
E aprop deslia aquel en le ters dia o en le quart, e prohibeys le malaute de anament per xl dias.	 "Take the first step on the third day or fourth, and prohibit them from doing so for another 10 days.
Mays si es forsat de anar denant aquel spazi, no es fayta segurtat que la dislocacio no sia sobre lu dissolvuda e corrumpuda, e aprop aquo que no recipia curacio.	 "If you are unable to perform the stretch regularly, ensure that the dislocation is not loose or deformed and make sure it has healed properly, in order to prevent any injury.
E si accideys a lu apostema caut, lahoras cove que tu aministre en la cedacio de lu aquo en lo qual precedic la nostra narracio, en autre loc de curacio e de embrocacio, entro que sia remauguda.	 "If the patient feels any pain during this stretch, proceed as described in our previous explanation and perform further care and application of treatments until it is cured.
Capitol .xxxiiii.	 When joint pain is caused by cold humors that infiltrate each part of the body, it is customarily called gout by doctors when the pain occurs in the feet.
De curacio de dislocacio dels ditz dels pes.	 To cure dislocated toes.
Cove que aquel qu’es dislocat sia engualhat am pauca extencio ses trebal; e aquo que no es dificil, abantz es leugier.	 If the dislocation is small, it can be easily fixed by a quick application of heat.
Mays si la dislocacio es en alcus nozes del dos del pe, lahoras cove que fassas cezer le malaute le sieu pe sobre loc engual de la terra o sobre taula, e sia estant ayssi cum si anava.	 If the dislocation is on both feet, then apply a cushion either over the ground or table to support it while standing in the same position as before.
E aprop tu sta de pes, e pausa le tieu pe sobre aquo que imineys de las juncturas, e aprop calca aquel am le tieu pe am vertut entro que retorne, e que vejas aquel ja engualhat e no aparesca en le loc eminencia.	 After you have put your foot down and place it over the points of the joints, then gently press that same foot against a spot near where they were, causing them to return to their original location and disappear from prominence.
E aprop pausa dejos le ventre del pe de lu una taula que prengua tot le pe, a la qual sian dos caps, e aprop strenh aquel am strectura decent e ferma per tres dias; e aprop deslia aquel e fay aquel repausar de ambulacio per motz dias, entro que sia estrenhut e de reddicio sia assegurat.	 After placing the foot on a flat surface and making it take up the whole of the foot with two heads, then stretch that same limb tightly for three days; after this, let it rest for seven days between medical treatments to ensure its safety and security.
Capitol .xxxv.	 This is the end of the translation.
De las specias de dislocacio que sian faytas am plagua o am fractura o am quascuna ensemps.	 Of joint dislocations that are caused by cold humors or tears, fractures, or any other type of injury.
Quan accideys alcuna causa de aquelas, e tu te perforssas en la curacio de aquela e en la restauracio de lu, motas veguadas succezeys la mort.	 If the cause is unknown and you are unable to cure or restore it then that will lead to death.
E per aquo no cove que sobre la curacio de lu presuma, sino aquel que es savi en l’art, de lonc uzatge, misericordios e pietados, tardiu, no-ardit ni presomptuos; e que use en le comensament de medicinas que cedan apostemas cautz tant solament, e leyssa le malaute al divinal jutgament, sino ad aquel al qual speras salut de perdicio, am de la malautia alleviacio, e en la qual appareys alcuna speransa.	 "In the meantime, do not expect immediate relief from pain caused by cold humors in a patient's joints; rather, it is advised to wait until the passage of time brings alleviation through compassion and kindness.
E adonc esforsa te tantost far de lu la reduccio en le comensament de la causa, denant que endevengua apostema caut.	 "But if you want to reduce it in the early stages, then ask for medical attention immediately.
E adonc si le membre retorna segon que volem, lahoras aministra regiment le qual ceda apostema caut e cura la plagua am aquo que conveneys a lu dels enguentz desiccatius.	 "Then once the member returns to you as desired, the doctor will provide treatment including cauterization and care for any resulting abscesses.
E si dislocacio es am fractura e accideys en le os satagias separadas, lahoras tu perforsa le stement de lor, e fay en aquo so que havem dit en las malautias simplas de aquo que es precedit en les locz de aquels.	 "If dislocation occurs and the bones are separated in such a way that they do not touch each other, you should seek treatment immediately.
E guarda e esquiva segon la tua vertut aquel del intrament en las vias de temor segon que a tu es precedida la mia predicacio; quar aquo es milhor a tu deves le tieu Creator, e mays permanent a la tua gloria, e mays saludos al tieu cos verays aquels en le tieu temps.	 "Be careful and avoid doing anything that might upset your faith or your trust in the One who preceded my prediction; for it is better to you than all of creation will endure its duration and will enjoy permanent glory, and more blessings on your Creator's face during this time.
Ayssi fineysso las paraulas de Albucasim perfieytament de las quals Dieus ne sia benezeyt.	 "These are the prayers of Abu Bakr that Allah may grant them mercy.
Amen.	 Amen
